  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d660bd73-5dfb-4a45-8ee0-fc016c0f2c8b'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/574391-looking-for-a-romance-maybe">Looking for a romance(maybe novella/prequel) about the heroine gets kidnapped by an oldlady kidnapped her to feed her vampire son, who she held captive in the basement. Every year the woman would kidnap someone for her son and let them go. First the she was scared, but they ended up falling in love and had sex. He erased her memory, but she got pregnant and remembered. Came back to rescue him after his mom died. Help?</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_574391'><a id="like_count_community_question_574391" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/574391?resource_type=CommunityQuestion"><span class="likesCount">1 like</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F5153799-father-mine">like</a></span>

  <span id="freeText12390593093679028088" style="display:none"><b>5 Swoon Z Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/9820387_zpszqmyhhar.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>First read 2014<br>Reread 4/2/2017<br><br><b>Spoilers</b><br><br><b>“You’re like your mahmen,” he whispered. “You make the world go away for me”-Z</b><br><br>OMG I can't take all the yumminess of Z. I've melted into a big puddle of goofy fangirl happy goo. To say this little bitty Novella was epic seems weak for the way it made me feel. This story was beautiful, moving, and totally nailed me in the feels. I loved every single minute of it. To read about Z and Bella having their problems after Nalla was born and work through them coming out stronger on the other side.....OMG it was heartwarming. Z was having a lot of problems with his pasts and Nalla and I loved how he turned it around and became a amazing father. I also loved him and Bella who had been having their own issues being able to be alone as a couple since the baby was born come together. And when they did there was enough heat to melt my kindle. Great read! Perfect! I want more Z, Bella, and Nalla, and I wish this one was longer!<br><br><b>"Have you missed my kisses, darling mate? The ones I like to give you between your thights?" "Yes," she choked out-Z and Bella</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/Fathermine_zpslfp9yvor.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>“Hey, what are you doing, little one? You want more? You are just too much . . . you . . . oh, no . . . not the quivering lip . . . oh, no.” Nalla let out a giggle. “Outrageous! You want more, and you know you’re going to get what you want because of The Lip. Jeez, you’ve got your father wrapped around your little finger, don’t you.” -Z and Bella</b></span>

    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer623286120" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7991915735002211893">5 ZSADIST STARS.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>"You are everything to me."</b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422732i/841498._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The heartbreaking tale of Zsadist and the ghosts of his past continue in this novella that to be honest I completely devoured. I loved having an 'extra' glimpse into the family life of Zsadist, Bella and their newborn, Nalla.<br/><br/>Zsadist is my favourite of the black dagger brotherhood, and it goes without saying that I was more than a little excited when I found out this short story was next in the line up.<br/><br/>So what's it about ...<br/>Well, like the title sugge</span>
  <span id="freeText7991915735002211893" style="display:none">5 ZSADIST STARS.<br><br><i>
  <b>"You are everything to me."</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422732i/841498._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The heartbreaking tale of Zsadist and the ghosts of his past continue in this novella that to be honest I completely devoured. I loved having an 'extra' glimpse into the family life of Zsadist, Bella and their newborn, Nalla.<br><br>Zsadist is my favourite of the black dagger brotherhood, and it goes without saying that I was more than a little excited when I found out this short story was next in the line up.<br><br>So what's it about ...<br>Well, like the title suggests this novella gives Brotherhood fans another delicious look-see into the lives of our favourite vampires. To set the scene, Zsadist and Bella have overcome the threat of pregnancy that has hung over their lives for months, here we get to experience the joy, sacrifice and pain of becoming parents and surviving the heartbreaking reality of Zsadist's past.<br><br>Utterly heartbreaking, with an intensity that can only come from a story about my favourite vamps, 'father mine' is an equally emotional and sensual story with a gorgeous ending ...<br><br>if like me your a brotherhood fan don't miss out on this short but compelling novella, you won't be disappointed.<br><br>5 HUGE STARS.</span>

Z was so worried the entire time Bella was pregnant because a lot of vampire females die in childbirth and she was already having a difficult pregnancy. Both he and Phury thought that if he lost Bella he wouldn’t have anything to live for. <br/><br/>Bella lived and had the baby, but afterward Zsadist wouldn’t go near the baby. He wouldn’t feed from Bella and was having horrible nightmares agai</span>
  <span id="freeText2246510196282349604" style="display:none"><strong>Gotta love a happy Z!</strong><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1577228614i/28664949._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was the story of Zsadist and his downward spiral after the birth of his daughter Nalla. Z was so worried the entire time Bella was pregnant because a lot of vampire females die in childbirth and she was already having a difficult pregnancy. Both he and Phury thought that if he lost Bella he wouldn’t have anything to live for. <br><br>Bella lived and had the baby, but afterward Zsadist wouldn’t go near the baby. He wouldn’t feed from Bella and was having horrible nightmares again about being a blood slave. This is the story of how he gets form that state to happy with his life and with his family. Zsadist is my favorite of all the brothers so it is great to finally see him get over all his pain and suffering and just finally be happy. <br><br><a href="https://www.ilikebooksbest.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a>|<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/wennel" rel="nofollow noopener">Goodreads</a>|<a href="https://www.facebook.com/ilikebooksbest" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>|<a href="https://smile.amazon.com/gp/profile/amzn1.account.AFFE5A2BGXJQTQMCYHFC4YHV6KFQ?preview=true" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a>|<a href="https://www.twitter.com/wendysu020202" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a>|<a href="https://www.bookbub.com/profile/1895823057" rel="nofollow noopener">BookBub</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer159721525654523294"><br/><b>***5 Stars***</b><br/><br/><u>
  <b>WARNING</b>
</u>: Spoilers ahead if you haven't read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42900.Lover_Awakened__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___3_' title='Lover Awakened (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #3) by J.R. Ward' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lover Awakened</a>.<br/><br/>After I finished Z's book, I just had to jump into this novella. Typically I have a hard time jumping around in a series, but there was no way I could pass up more Zsadist and Bella. <br/><br/>The novella provided a fantastic look into their lives. The struggles of adjusting to their new family, Z's apprehension and fear of dirtying his beautifully pure daughter, all his demons coming back full force with the realization that she'</span>
  <span id="freeText159721525654523294" style="display:none"><br><b>***5 Stars***</b><br><br><u>
  <b>WARNING</b>
</u>: Spoilers ahead if you haven't read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42900.Lover_Awakened__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___3_" title="Lover Awakened (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #3) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Awakened</a>.<br><br>After I finished Z's book, I just had to jump into this novella. Typically I have a hard time jumping around in a series, but there was no way I could pass up more Zsadist and Bella. <br><br>The novella provided a fantastic look into their lives. The struggles of adjusting to their new family, Z's apprehension and fear of dirtying his beautifully pure daughter, all his demons coming back full force with the realization that she'll have questions about his appearance when she gets older. <br><br>We also see Bella's insecurities after giving birth. She is now a devoted mother, but unsure of her footing as she feels Z pulling away from both their daughter and her. She knows he loves her, but she's been through so much emotionally and physically. Does he see her differently now? As much as she's understanding of his issues, she now needs some reassurances herself. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"You are just as beautiful as the first time I saw you in the gym all those nights and days ago. You stopped my heart then - just froze it in my chest. And you stop it now."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>I loved watching these two work through their issues. They're so open and loving. So supportive of each other. Bella listens to Z's heartbreaking confessions with understanding and a sympathetic heart, while Zsadist is able to understand that although he thought the distance was better for his shellan and Nalla, ultimately what they truly need is him. Just him, as he is. All his scars. All his fears. All his love. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381200445ra/4512081.gif" width="500" height="209" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"They were both his, these two. His and his alone, and he had to take care of them. One was his heart and the other a piece of himself, and they completed him by filling voids he didn't know he had."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1888824991984084223">This is a must read if you loved <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42900.Lover_Awakened__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___3_' title='Lover Awakened (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #3) by J.R. Ward' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lover Awakened</a>. Z and Bella are still my favorite couple to date. They have issues and struggles. It makes them more relatable, more realistic. To me, their story will never end. Ward could write three more books about them and I guarantee that they would be just as touching and beautifully written as the first.<br/><br/>Speaking of the writing, it was wonderful. I could quote the whole book. Every line was filled with emotion. It was perfect.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>I’m so sorry. I love you. P</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText1888824991984084223" style="display:none">This is a must read if you loved <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42900.Lover_Awakened__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___3_" title="Lover Awakened (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #3) by J.R.   <b>I’m so sorry. I love you. Please forgive me. Can’t live without you.</b>
</i><br><br>I also loved seeing the shellans play a role in this book. Mary and Doc Jane were just as wonderful as Bella and Z. Seeing them help Z was heartwarming. I loved Jane's tough love. <br><br><b>
  <i>Here's my deal. Wrath's appointed me as the Brotherhood's personal physician. You screw around with eating and feeding and sleeping such that it impairs your performance, I will bench your ass.</i>

He has to come to terms with his past and embrace his future. The obstacles are great, the journey is paved with sorrow, and yet at the end of the path is pure and complete joy! The feels are immense! <br><br><b>“I love you . . .” he whispered. “Please don’t leave me.” </b><br><br>Bella and Z are by far my favorite BDB couple. I absolutely adored this novella. <div id="review_175896218" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/175896218" />
    <a title="When Funmi Met Romance" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance"><img alt="When Funmi Met Romance" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572219419p2/5615242.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/175896218?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="When Funmi Met Romance" class="user" itemprop="url" name="When Funmi Met Romance" href="/user/show/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance">When Funmi Met Romance</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Zsadist and Bella Fanatics</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=great-sex">great-sex</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=battle">battle</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer175896218" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3631511775594260756"> Reread: I really am in a novel nostalgic mood because I keep rereading books that are my favorite. I almost never really reread. Not to mention, I'm not a fan of J.R.Ward, in fact I don't like her books. However, Zsadist and Bella captured the hell out of my heart. Their book is like the pinnacle of a tortured hero redemption book. Its one of the best stories I have ever read. This little novella just cemented that belief. I love how JR keeps it real. Zsadist and Bella have a hell of a time try</span>
  <span id="freeText3631511775594260756" style="display:none"> Reread: I really am in a novel nostalgic mood because I keep rereading books that are my favorite. I almost never really reread. Not to mention, I'm not a fan of J.R.Ward, in fact I don't like her books. However, Zsadist and Bella captured the hell out of my heart. Their book is like the pinnacle of a tortured hero redemption book. Its one of the best stories I have ever read. This little novella just cemented that belief. I love how JR keeps it real. Zsadist and Bella have a hell of a time trying to achieve happiness but somehow they do. Although this book is way unrealistic and can never manifest itself into reality, at the core it speaks to me. Its speaks volumes about how people are so much stronger than they know. People can get through the toughest times, and though its hard, happiness is attainable. Loveeee this story<br /><br />First read; June 25, 2011<br /><br /> This little novella at best was amazing. J.R.Ward is a one of a kind writer. Her books are akin to movies only twice as stimulating. I literally feel the emotion she writes as my stomach wretches during the intense scenes and my heart flutters at the love. I could go on and on but chances are if you read this amazing little short story you are well aware of the talented Ward, and this galacticly amazing couple she created. <br /> Zsadist and Bella are in my opinion so beautiful, and so real, i can dang near see them. I see them and their life clearer than any romance book. Often, romance books give you a hazy picture of everything in your mind. However, Ward's Zsadist and Bella's life is like watching a blu ray movie on a Digital High Definition Flat Plasma Screan TV. Its clear as day. Many times in Romance, heroines and heroes go through hell and high waters but are all peachy keen in the end. However, Ward has penned a couple that is glaringly imperfect and a product of their torturous past. Yet, she writes a realistic Happily Ever After. This little short gives the readers so much closure and pleasure. I have no doubt that anyone reading this is craaaaazy emotionally invested in Zsadist and Bella. I know I am, to the point of absurdity. <br /><br />It sucks though, Ward has created the only Romance Couple that I want to have a never ending series. I could read about the small nuances of Zsadist and Bella's life forever. Everything between them is special, from eating, to showers, to laughs. I know this is meant to give closure, but when a person creates such a perfect couple there is no such thing as closure. Great story, will be read, and reread, until the corners of the internet pages are worn in my kindle :p</span>

          </span>

    <a title="Jamie (TheRebelliousReader)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7515832-jamie-therebelliousreader"><img alt="Jamie (TheRebelliousReader)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604020630p2/7515832.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2259725722?book_show_action=true">Jan 15, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jamie (TheRebelliousReader)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jamie (TheRebelliousReader)" href="/user/show/7515832-jamie-therebelliousreader">Jamie (TheRebelliousReader)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/29968195-father-mine">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7515832-jamie-therebelliousreader?shelf=favorite-book-couple">favorite-book-couple</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7515832-jamie-therebelliousreader?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2259725722" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12393558949414327568">5 stars. This was absolutely beautiful. J.R Ward managed to get me emotional in less than 100 pages. Brava!<br/><br/>It goes without saying that Zsadist has been my favorite character since the beginning so I was really excited to read this. But I'm not going to lie, I have never wanted to slap the hell out of Z as much as I did at the beginning of this story. I understood his reasoning and his fears, yes, but that detachment made my blood boil I was so angry with him. I felt terrible for Bella and Nalla.</span>
  <span id="freeText12393558949414327568" style="display:none">5 stars. This was absolutely beautiful. J.R Ward managed to get me emotional in less than 100 pages. Brava!<br /><br />It goes without saying that Zsadist has been my favorite character since the beginning so I was really excited to read this. But I'm not going to lie, I have never wanted to slap the hell out of Z as much as I did at the beginning of this story. I understood his reasoning and his fears, yes, but that detachment made my blood boil I was so angry with him. I felt terrible for Bella and Nalla. I just wanted to shake him and tell him to get his ish together! Bella is a trooper and such an amazing character. Kudos to her for sticking it out cause I would've lost my mind.<br /><br />Then of course in typical Ward fashion, she flipped it around and fixed it and even managed to make me cry in the end. Bella and Z have such a wonderful relationship and it kinda sucked seeing them go through their grievances but I feel like it definitely made them stronger and brought them closer together.<br /><br />Listen, Z bonding with baby Nalla was almost the death of me. It was everything. My heart hurts from all the cuteness.<br /><br />Also, side note but I appreciated all of the Rhage appearances in this because lord knows he doesn't show up nearly enough for my taste in the series so that was an added bonus.<br /><br />Overall, do I think this is a necessary read? Um, hell yes absolutely! Especially if you're a fan of Z. It's further development for his character and that's always a plus. <br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="12393558949414327568" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1945375796078674313">Okay, so I alread said that Z is my fave...and that his book is well worth reading. This story falls in that same realm. Father Mine takes place after the last chapter of Lover Awakened, but before the epiloge. This is the story of how Z continues to grew as a person now that Bella has given birth to their daughter.   <span id="freeText1945375796078674313" style="display:none">Okay, so I alread said that Z is my fave...and that his book is well worth reading. This story falls in that same realm. Father Mine takes place after the last chapter of Lover Awakened, but before the epiloge. This is the story of how Z continues to grew as a person now that Bella has given birth to their daughter. He goes through the same issues of self doubt in being a good and caring father. So much so that he avoids his daughter, thinking it would be better that she didn't know his past and how "damaged" he is. Bella helps him again in finding peace with himself. This is a short story, but ends on such a high note, it will warm your heart. </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer104736560" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12539299887160791404">I've actually read this from the<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2880715.The_Black_Dagger_Brotherhood_An_Insider_s_Guide' title='The Black Dagger Brotherhood An Insider's Guide by J.R. Ward' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1275640178s/2880715.jpg' alt='The Black Dagger Brotherhood An Insider's Guide by J.R. Ward' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a>which I'm currently reading right now but I'd already finished the Father Mine story.<br/><br/>I'd like to say that if you'd love Zsadist you'd definitely love this. I don't know if I'm weird or I'm just really weird that when it came to Z I felt that my heart was melting every time I've read about his struggles and how he's so tortured on the inside. And honestly I did cry on this book, really what's wrong with me? o.O I'm not really a usual crier so that's really is s</span>
  <span id="freeText12539299887160791404" style="display:none">I've actually read this from the<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2880715.The_Black_Dagger_Brotherhood_An_Insider_s_Guide" title="The Black Dagger Brotherhood An Insider's Guide by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1275640178s/2880715.jpg" alt="The Black Dagger Brotherhood An Insider's Guide by J.R. Ward" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>which I'm currently reading right now but I'd already finished the Father Mine story.<br><br>I'd like to say that if you'd love Zsadist you'd definitely love this. I don't know if I'm weird or I'm just really weird that when it came to Z I felt that my heart was melting every time I've read about his struggles and how he's so tortured on the inside. And honestly I did cry on this book, really what's wrong with me? o.O I'm not really a usual crier so that's really is something.<br><br>I'd also want to say that the conflict and the struggles between Bella and Z are really realistic, it's not over the top and I think even if it's fictional, it's something that is also could translate in our world. Like the post-partum depression it's pretty much the same with the ones that we've been studying on my nursing classes. Like after pregnancy the woman feels very insecure with the changes that her body goes through and to combat the depression, the husband must support his wife by telling her she's still beautiful blah blah blah and appreciate her more and saying things like you look awful/ugly after the pregnancy is a big NO.<br><br>So much for that I also love the part when there's like a repeat of the Epilogue of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42900.Lover_Awakened__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___3_" title="Lover Awakened (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #3) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1169957160s/42900.jpg" alt="Lover Awakened (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #3) by J.R. Ward" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> but now it's on Bella's perspective is also cool. I also love the part that somehow Mary has also a part to Z's healing because she's been his counselor and all that. I also love Nalla, she's just so cute and cuddly, just want to like cuddle her in my arms. I just hope that we can get a story/ book where Nalla is all grown up and finding a guy that she love or something like that.<br><br>All in all it's a good story and highly recommended.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nXSWpFjpGAeBP+Rd2K6mwtGfEn2mRFw5/sBAutHLGHJTqRrLNNKQAb/IA2v4j/W75Nzj5+IC+/cHJqBPaJuIkQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }
